# Build up toward the World Revolution
country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr1.1
    title = chaosx.nr1.1.t
    desc = chaosx.nr1.1.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_stalin_propaganda

    is_triggered_only = yes
    major = yes

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            set_temp_variable = { base_value = 0.10 }
            set_temp_variable = { base_add = 0.02 }
            modify_value_based_on_chaos_tier = yes
            add_popularity = {
                ideology = communism
                popularity = var:modified_value
            }
            set_global_flag = communism_spread
        }
    }

    option = {
        trigger = {
            NOT = { has_government = communism }
        }
        name = chaosx.nr1.1.a
        effect_tooltip = {
            add_popularity = {
                ideology = communism
                popularity = var:modified_value
            }
        }
    }
    option = {
        trigger = {
            has_government = communism
        }
        name = chaosx.nr1.1.b
        effect_tooltip = {
            add_popularity = {
                ideology = communism
                popularity = var:modified_value
            }
        }
    }
}


# Communist strikes; damage to buildings. Build up toward the World Revolution
country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr1.2
    title = chaosx.nr1.2.t
    desc = chaosx.nr1.2.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_FIN_helsinki_bombed

    trigger = {
        NOT = { has_government = communism }
        communism > 0.10
        has_global_flag = communism_spread
    }

    mean_time_to_happen = {
        days = 20 # base mean time 1(100%)/days
    }

    option = { # OK, do nothing
        name = chaosx.nr1.2.a
        ai_chance = { base = 80 }
        custom_effect_tooltip = chaosx_tt_1_2a
        hidden_effect = {
            set_temp_variable = { state_population_percent = -0.001 } # 0.1% of state population
            set_temp_variable = { buildings_to_damage_per_state = 3 }
            set_temp_variable = { damage_modifier = 0.25 }
            set_temp_variable = { percent_of_states_to_target = 0.1 }
            damage_buildings_in_random_states = yes
        }
    }

    option = { # Try to subdue the strikes
        name = chaosx.nr1.2.b
        ai_chance = {
            base = 20
            # More likely to suppress strikes if:
            modifier = {
                add = 10
                has_war = yes # At war
            }
            modifier = {
                add = 10
                has_stability < 0.2 # Very low stability
            }
            modifier = {
                add = 50
                communism < 0.12 # Low communist support
            }
            # Less likely if:
            modifier = {
                factor = 0.5
                has_manpower < 10000 # Can't afford manpower loss
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 0.25
                communism > 0.3 # High communist support
            }
        }
        add_stability = -0.02
        add_political_power = -20
        add_manpower = -5000
        add_popularity = {
            ideology = communism
            popularity = -0.02
        }
    }
}


##############################################################################################################




# Workers strike communism uprising; Civil war
country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr1.3
    title = chaosx.nr1.3.t
    desc = chaosx.nr1.3.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_worker_protests

    trigger = {
        has_civil_war = no
        NOT = { has_government = communism }
        communism > 0.4
        has_global_flag = communism_spread
        has_stability < 0.2
    }

    mean_time_to_happen = {
        days = 150 # base mean time 1(100%)/days
    }

    option = { # Cool down the situation
        name = chaosx.nr1.3.a
        ai_chance = {
            base = 33
        }
        add_war_support = -0.10
        add_stability = -0.10
        add_political_power = -100
        add_popularity = {
            ideology = communism
            popularity = -0.05
        }
    }

    option = { # Start civil war
        name = chaosx.nr1.3.b
        ai_chance = {
            base = 34
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                communism > 0.6
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 0.25
                has_war = yes
            }

        }
        add_war_support = 0.10
        add_political_power = 100
        hidden_effect = {
            set_temp_variable = { communist_civil_war_size = party_popularity@communism }
            if = { limit = { check_variable = { communist_civil_war_size > 0.6 } } set_temp_variable = { communist_civil_war_size = 0.6 } }
        }
        start_civil_war = {
            ideology = communism
            size = var:communist_civil_war_size
        }
        hidden_effect = {
            add_popularity = {
                ideology = communism
                popularity = -0.5
            }
        }
    }

    option = { # Give up
        name = chaosx.nr1.3.c
        ai_chance = {
            base = 33
            modifier = {
                factor = 2
                communism > 0.6
            }
        }
        add_stability = -0.20
        add_ruling_to_com = yes
        set_politics = {
            ruling_party = communism
            elections_allowed = no
        }
    }
}

# TODO: Make zombies more realistic: Diplomatic actions should be limited, no alliances, no factions, no diplomacy, no trade, no lend lease, no volunteers, no military access, no peace deals. Zombies should have hostile relations with every country. The generals should be zombies. Basically remove anything human about them. The more danger there is, the more intelligent the zombies are and the more technology they can use. Also zombies become more powerful. Maybe make it so that zombies are weaker during day and stronger during the night. Zombies must attack no matter what, they can't stay idle. Even if offensive is likely unsuccessful, they should still attack.
country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr2.1
    title = chaosx.nr2.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            random_state = {
                limit = { is_island_state = no state_population_k > 1000 NOT = { is_controlled_by = ZZZ } } # At least 1 million
                save_global_event_target_as = zombie_state
                transfer_state_to = ZZZ # Sets ZZZ owner of the state
                add_core_of = ZZZ
                ZZZ = {
                    load_oob = "ZZZ_1936" # Get Brainzz Horde template
                }
                create_unit = {
                    division = "name = \"Brainzz Horde\" division_template = \"Brainzz Horde\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
                    count = 10
                    owner = ZZZ
                }
            }

            ZZZ = {
                add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
                    type = infantry_equipment
                    amount = 1000 # Since Zombies require 1 piece of equipment to deploy a division
                    producer = CHI
                }
            }

            if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = has_zombie_outbreak } }
                set_global_flag = has_zombie_outbreak
            }

        }
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr2.3

    trigger = {
        has_global_flag = has_zombie_outbreak
        is_ai = no
    }

    mean_time_to_happen = {
        days = 10
    }

    fire_only_once = yes
    hidden = yes

    immediate = {
        play_song = "zombies"

        set_global_flag = {
            flag = super_event_visible
            days = 30
            value = 1
        }
    }
}

country_event = { # Cure activated
    id = chaosx.nr2.2
    title = chaosx.nr2.2.t
    desc = chaosx.nr2.2.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_generic_research_lab

    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        effect_tooltip = {
            if = { limit = { is_in_tech_sharing_group = cure_sharing }
            add_timed_idea = {
                idea = cure_activated
                days = 120
            }
        } else = {
            add_timed_idea = {
                idea = cure_activated
                days = 360
            }
        }
    }
    name = chaosx.nr2.2.a
}
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr3.1
    title = chaosx.nr3.1.t

    is_triggered_only = yes

    hidden = yes

    immediate = {
        if = { limit = { OR = { BHU = { is_ai = no } TIB = { is_ai = no } NEP = { is_ai = no } } }
        country_event = { id = chaosx.nr3.2 days = 1 }
    } else = {
        random_country = {
            limit = { OR = { tag = BHU tag = TIB tag = NEP } }
            country_event = { id = chaosx.nr3.2 days = 1 }
        }
    }
}
}


##############################################################################################################


country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr3.2
    title = chaosx.nr3.2.t
    desc = chaosx.nr3.2.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_lhasa

    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr3.2.a
        ai_chance = { base = 100 }
        hidden_effect = {
            set_cosmetic_tag = THR
            add_ideas = THR_gods_plan
            create_faction = gods_plan
            set_politics = {
                ruling_party = neutrality
                elections_allowed = no
                election_frequency = 48
                long_name = "God's Plan"
                name = "God's Plan"
            }
            add_popularity = {
                ideology = neutrality
                popularity = 1.00
            }
            retire_country_leader = yes
            create_country_leader = {
                name = "God"
                picture = GFX_portrait_THR_godly_figure
                ideology = despotism
            }
            news_event = { id = chaosx.news.9 days = 3 }
        }
        BHU = {
            if = { limit = { NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
            country_event = { id = chaosx.nr3.3 days = 3 }
            every_core_state = {
                add_core_of = ROOT
            }
        }
    }
    NEP = {
        if = { limit = { NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
        country_event = { id = chaosx.nr3.3 days = 1 }
        every_core_state = {
            add_core_of = ROOT
        }
    }
}
TIB = {
    if = { limit = { NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
    country_event = { id = chaosx.nr3.3 days = 2 }
    every_core_state = {
        add_core_of = ROOT
    }
}
}
}
option = {
    name = chaosx.nr3.2.b
    add_stability = -0.10
    ai_chance = { base = 0 }
}
}


##############################################################################################################


country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr3.3
    title = chaosx.nr3.3.t
    desc = chaosx.nr3.3.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_lhasa

    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr3.3.a
        ai_chance = { base = 70 }
        FROM = {
            annex_country = {
                target = ROOT
                transfer_troops = yes
            }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr3.3.b
        add_stability = -0.10
        add_war_support = 0.10
        FROM = {
            create_wargoal = {
                target = ROOT
                type = annex_everything
            }
        }
        ai_chance = { base = 30 }
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr4.1
    title = chaosx.nr4.1.t

    hidden = yes

    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        random_country = {
            random_other_country = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = PREV } }
                declare_war_on = {
                    type = annex_everything
                    target = PREV
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

        SOV = {
            release = UKR
            release = BLR
        }

    }

}

#   ### #    # #####  ###### #      ###### #    # #####  ###### #    #  ####  ######    #    # #    #   ##   ######

##############################################################################################################



country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr6.1
    title = chaosx.nr6.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        clear_array = global.indp_countries
        every_possible_country = {
            limit = { exists = no any_state = { is_core_of = PREV } NOT = { OR = { tag = UKR tag = BEL } } }
            random_select_amount = 3
            add_to_array = { global.indp_countries = THIS }
        }
        for_each_scope_loop = {
            array = global.indp_countries
            random_country = {
                limit = { any_controlled_state = { is_core_of = PREV.PREV } }
                release = PREV
                set_truce = {
                    target = PREV
                    days = 180
                }
                PREV = { # So that the country doesn't lose cores
                    every_owned_state = {
                        add_core_of = PREV.PREV
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        set_variable = { global.indp_country_1 = global.indp_countries^0 }
        set_variable = { global.indp_country_2 = global.indp_countries^1 }
        set_variable = { global.indp_country_3 = global.indp_countries^2 }
        news_event = { id = chaosx.news.6 days = 2 }
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr7.1
    title = chaosx.nr7.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        random_country = {
            limit = { all_owned_state = { is_island_state = no } }
            country_event = { id = chaosx.nr7.2 days = 1 }
        }
    }
}


##############################################################################################################


country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr7.2
    title = chaosx.nr7.2.t
    desc = chaosx.nr7.2.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_army_training

    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            clear_variable = num_neighbors
            clear_array = selected_neighbors
            every_neighbor_country = {
                limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ROOT.selected_neighbors = THIS.id } } }
                random_select_amount = 4
                add_to_variable = { ROOT.num_neighbors = 1 }
                add_to_array = { ROOT.selected_neighbors = THIS.id }
            }
            log = "Number of neighbors [ROOT.GetName] has: [?num_neighbors|.0]"
        }
    }

    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr7.2.a
        add_war_support = 0.10
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 10
            modifier = {
                add = 50
                var:selected_neighbors^0 = {
                    is_major = no
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                add = 20
                var:selected_neighbors^0 = {
                    has_war = yes
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                add = 20
                var:selected_neighbors^0 = { num_divisions < ROOT.num_divisions }
            }
        }
        var:selected_neighbors^0 = {
            ROOT = {
                declare_war_on = {
                    type = annex_everything
                    target = PREV
                }
            }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr7.2.b
        add_war_support = 0.10
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 10
            modifier = {
                add = 50
                var:selected_neighbors^1 = {
                    is_major = no
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                add = 20
                var:selected_neighbors^1 = {
                    has_war = yes
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                add = 20
                var:selected_neighbors^1 = { num_divisions < ROOT.num_divisions }
            }
        }
        var:selected_neighbors^1 = {
            ROOT = {
                declare_war_on = {
                    type = annex_everything
                    target = PREV
                }
            }
        }
        trigger = {
            check_variable = { num_neighbors > 1 }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr7.2.c
        add_war_support = 0.10
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 10
            modifier = {
                add = 50
                var:selected_neighbors^2 = {
                    is_major = no
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                add = 20
                var:selected_neighbors^2 = {
                    has_war = yes
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                add = 20
                var:selected_neighbors^2 = { num_divisions < ROOT.num_divisions }
            }
        }
        var:selected_neighbors^2 = {
            ROOT = {
                declare_war_on = {
                    type = annex_everything
                    target = PREV
                }
            }
        }
        trigger = {
            check_variable = { num_neighbors > 2 }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr7.2.e
        add_war_support = 0.10
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 10
            modifier = {
                add = 50
                var:selected_neighbors^3 = {
                    is_major = no
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                add = 20
                var:selected_neighbors^3 = {
                    has_war = yes
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                add = 20
                var:selected_neighbors^3 = { num_divisions < ROOT.num_divisions }
            }
        }
        var:selected_neighbors^3 = {
            ROOT = {
                declare_war_on = {
                    type = annex_everything
                    target = PREV
                }
            }
        }
        trigger = {
            check_variable = { num_neighbors > 3 }
        }
    }
}

        }
    }

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr10.2
    title = chaosx.nr10.2.t
    desc = chaosx.nr10.2.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_war_or_peace

    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr10.2.a
        news_event = { id = chaosx.news.7 days = 4 }
        ai_chance = { base = 50 }
        add_war_support = 1.00
        add_stability = -0.1
        add_political_power = 100
        add_ideas = symbol_of_war
        every_other_country = {
            limit = { is_subject = no }
            country_event = { id = chaosx.nr10.3 days = 2 }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr10.2.b
        news_event = { id = chaosx.news.8 days = 4 }
        add_stability = 1.00
        add_war_support = -0.1
        add_political_power = 100
        add_ideas = symbol_of_peace
        every_other_country = {
            limit = { is_subject = no }
            country_event = { id = chaosx.nr10.4 days = 2 }
        }
        ai_chance = { base = 50 }
    }
    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr10.2.c
        add_stability = -0.1
        add_war_support = -0.1
        add_political_power = -100
        ai_chance = { base = 0 }
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr10.3
    title = chaosx.nr10.3.t
    desc = chaosx.nr10.3.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_tur_machine_gunners

    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr10.3.a
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 50
            modifier = {
                add = 50
                FROM = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
            }
        }
        if = { limit = { FROM = { has_government = fascism } }
        add_popularity = {
            ideology = fascism
            popularity = 0.20
        }
    } else_if = { limit = { FROM = { has_government = democratic } }
    add_popularity = {
        ideology = democratic
        popularity = 0.20
    }
} else_if = { limit = { FROM = { has_government = neutrality } }
add_popularity = {
    ideology = neutrality
    popularity = 0.20
}
} else_if = { limit = { FROM = { has_government = communism } }
add_popularity = {
    ideology = communism
    popularity = 0.20
}
}
add_war_support = 0.1
add_political_power = 100
effect_tooltip = {
    FROM = {
        add_political_power = 25
        add_stability = 0.02
        add_war_support = 0.02
    }
}
FROM = {
    country_event = { id = chaosx.nr10.5 days = 1 }
}
add_opinion_modifier = {
    target = FROM
    modifier = small_increase
}
}
option = {
    name = chaosx.nr10.3.b
    add_stability = 0.05
    effect_tooltip = {
        FROM = {
            add_political_power = -10
            add_stability = -0.02
            add_war_support = -0.02
        }
    }
    FROM = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr10.6 days = 1 } }
    add_opinion_modifier = {
        target = FROM
        modifier = unstable_alliance
    }
    ai_chance = {
        factor = 50
        modifier = {
            add = 50
            FROM = { is_enemy_ideology = yes }
        }
        modifier = {
            add = 20
            FROM = { num_of_factories < ROOT.num_of_factories }
        }
        modifier = {
            add = 50
            ROOT = { is_major = yes }
        }
    }
}
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr11.1
    title = chaosx.nr11.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        random_other_country = {
            declare_war_on = {
                target = ROOT
                type = annex_everything
            }
            random_other_country = {
                declare_war_on = {
                    target = ROOT
                    type = annex_everything
                }
                random_other_country = {
                    create_faction = anti_player_pact
                    add_to_faction = PREV.PREV
                    add_to_faction = PREV
                    declare_war_on = {
                        target = ROOT
                        type = annex_everything
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        country_event = { id = chaosx.nr11.2 days = 1 }
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr12.1
    title = chaosx.nr12.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        if = { limit = { ROOT = { is_ai = no capital_scope = { is_on_continent = africa } } }
        country_event = { id = chaosx.nr12.2 days = 1 }
    } else = {
        random_country = {
            limit = { capital_scope = { is_on_continent = africa } }
            country_event = { id = chaosx.nr12.2 days = 1 }
        }
    }
}
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr12.2
    title = chaosx.nr12.2.t
    desc = chaosx.nr12.2.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_generic_african_unity

    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        ai_chance = { base = 90 }
        name = chaosx.nr12.2.a
        if = { limit = { tag = SAF is_subject = yes }
        overlord = {
            set_autonomy = {
                target = SAF
                autonomous_state = autonomy_free
                end_wars = yes
                end_civil_wars = yes
            }
        }
    }
    leave_faction = yes
    set_cosmetic_tag = AFR
    add_ideas = AFR_african_ambission
    set_politics = {
        ruling_party = neutrality
        elections_allowed = no
        election_frequency = 48
        long_name = "Absolute Monarchy of King of Africa"
        name = "African Dynasty"
    }
    add_popularity = {
        ideology = neutrality
        popularity = 1.00
    }
    retire_country_leader = yes
    create_country_leader = {
        name = "King of Africa"
        picture = GFX_portrait_AFR_king_of_africa
        expire = "1965.1.1"
        ideology = despotism
    }
    every_state = {
        limit = { is_on_continent = africa }
        add_core_of = ROOT
    }
    division_template = {
        name = "African Tribal Division"
        regiments = {
            irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
            irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
            irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
            irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 3 }
            irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
            irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
            irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
            irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 3 }
            irregular_infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
            irregular_infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
            irregular_infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
            irregular_infantry = { x = 2 y = 3 }
            irregular_infantry = { x = 3 y = 0 }
            irregular_infantry = { x = 3 y = 1 }
            irregular_infantry = { x = 3 y = 2 }
            irregular_infantry = { x = 3 y = 3 }
        }
    }
    capital_scope = {
        create_unit = {
            division = "name = \"African Tribes\" division_template = \"African Tribal Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
            count = 10
            owner = ROOT
        }
    }
    every_other_country = {
        limit = { any_owned_state = { is_on_continent = africa } }
        country_event = { id = chaosx.nr12.3 days = 1 }
    }
    news_event = { id = chaosx.news.10 days = 4 }
}
option = {
    ai_chance = { base = 10 }
    add_stability = -0.1
    name = chaosx.nr12.2.b
}
}


##############################################################################################################


country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr12.3
    title = chaosx.nr12.3.t
    desc = chaosx.nr12.3.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_generic_african_unity

    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 5
            modifier = {
                add = 25
                capital_scope = { is_on_continent = africa }
            }
        }
        add_stability = -0.1
        add_political_power = -50
        name = chaosx.nr12.3.a
        ROOT = {
            if = { limit = { capital_scope = { is_on_continent = africa } }
            FROM = {
                annex_country = {
                    target = ROOT
                    transfer_troops = yes
                }
            }
        } else = {
            every_state = {
                limit = { is_on_continent = africa is_controlled_by = ROOT }
                transfer_state_to = FROM
            }
        }

    }

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr13.1
    title = chaosx.nr13.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        random_country = {
            random_list = {
                10 = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr13.2 days = 1 } } # Earthquake
                10 = { if = { limit = { any_owned_state = { is_coastal = yes } }
                country_event = { id = chaosx.nr13.3 days = 1 } # Flood
            } else = {
                country_event = { id = chaosx.nr13.2 days = 1 }
            }
        }
        10 = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr13.4 days = 1 } } # Tornado
        10 = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr13.5 days = 1 } } # Wildfire
        10 = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr13.6 days = 1 } } # Lightning Storm
        10 = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr13.7 days = 1 } } # Hurricane
    }
}
}
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr17.2
    title = chaosx.nr17.2.t
    desc = chaosx.nr17.2.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_generic_research_lab

    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr17.2.a
        set_variable = { global.joined_faction_leader = GER }
        trigger = {
            GER = { is_faction_leader = yes }
        }
        GER = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 100
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                NOT = { has_government = fascism }
            }
        }
        news_event = { id = chaosx.news.4 days = 2 }
    }
    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr17.2.b
        set_variable = { global.joined_faction_leader = SOV }
        trigger = {
            SOV = { is_faction_leader = yes }
        }
        SOV = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 100
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                NOT = { has_government = communism }
            }
        }
        news_event = { id = chaosx.news.4 days = 2 }
    }
    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr17.2.e
        set_variable = { global.joined_faction_leader = ENG }
        trigger = {
            ENG = { is_faction_leader = yes }
        }
        ENG = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 100
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                NOT = { has_government = democratic }
            }
        }
        news_event = { id = chaosx.news.4 days = 2 }
    }
    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr17.2.c
        trigger = {
            any_country = { is_faction_leader = yes NOT = { OR = { tag = ENG tag = SOV tag = GER } } }
        }
        random_country = {
            limit = { is_faction_leader = yes NOT = { OR = { tag = ENG tag = SOV tag = GER } } }
            set_variable = { global.joined_faction_leader = THIS.id }
            THIS = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
        }
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 100
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                NOT = { has_government = neutrality }
            }
        }
        news_event = { id = chaosx.news.4 days = 2 }
    }
}

                            amount = 200

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr19.1
    title = chaosx.nr19.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        every_country = {
            division_template = {
                name = "Infantry Division"
                regiments = {
                    infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
                    infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
                    infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
                    infantry = { x = 0 y = 3 }
                    infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
                    infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
                    infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
                    infantry = { x = 1 y = 3 }
                }
            }
            every_controlled_state = {
                limit = { is_fully_controlled_by = PREV impassable = no }
                create_unit = {
                    division = "name = \"Random Events Division\" division_template = \"Infantry Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
                    owner = PREV
                }
            }
            country_event = { id = chaosx.nr19.2 days = 1 }
        }
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr20.1
    title = chaosx.nr20.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            random_list = {
                10 = {
                    set_variable = { global.black_death_continent = 1 }
                    every_country = {
                        limit = { capital_scope = { is_on_continent = europe } }
                        add_timed_idea = {
                            idea = black_death
                            days = 365
                        }
                    }
                } 10 = {
                    set_variable = { global.black_death_continent = 2 }
                    every_country = {
                        limit = { capital_scope = { is_on_continent = middle_east } }
                        add_timed_idea = {
                            idea = black_death
                            days = 365
                        }
                    }
                } 10 = {
                    set_variable = { global.black_death_continent = 3 }
                    every_country = {
                        limit = { capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia } }
                        add_timed_idea = {
                            idea = black_death
                            days = 365
                        }
                    }
                } 10 = {
                    set_variable = { global.black_death_continent = 4 }
                    every_country = {
                        limit = { capital_scope = { is_on_continent = africa } }
                        add_timed_idea = {
                            idea = black_death
                            days = 365
                        }
                    }
                } 10 = {
                    set_variable = { global.black_death_continent = 5 }
                    every_country = {
                        limit = { capital_scope = { is_on_continent = australia } }
                        add_timed_idea = {
                            idea = black_death
                            days = 365
                        }
                    }
                } 10 = {
                    set_variable = { global.black_death_continent = 6 }
                    every_country = {
                        limit = { capital_scope = { is_on_continent = north_america } }
                        add_timed_idea = {
                            idea = black_death
                            days = 365
                        }
                    }
                } 10 = {
                    set_variable = { global.black_death_continent = 7 }
                    every_country = {
                        limit = { capital_scope = { is_on_continent = south_america } }
                        add_timed_idea = {
                            idea = black_death
                            days = 365
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            news_event = { id = chaosx.news.21 days = 2 }
        }
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr26.1
    title = chaosx.nr26.1.t

    hidden = yes

    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        if = { limit = { any_owned_state = { is_desert_state = yes } }
        country_event = { id = chaosx.nr26.2 days = 1 }
    } else = {
        random_country = {
            limit = { num_of_factories > 50 any_owned_state = { is_desert_state = yes } }
            country_event = { id = chaosx.nr26.2 days = 1 }
        }
    }
}
}


##############################################################################################################


country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr26.2
    title = chaosx.nr26.2.t
    desc = chaosx.nr26.2.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_desert

    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        ai_chance = { base = 100 }
        name = chaosx.nr26.2.a
        hidden_effect = {
            every_owned_state = { limit = { is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT is_desert_state = yes }
            add_to_temp_array = { owned_desert_states = THIS }
        }
        for_each_loop = {
            array = owned_desert_states
            value = v
            add_to_temp_variable = { num_of_owned_desert_states = 1 } # Distribute factories evenly throughout states.
            log = "[ROOT.GetName] owns desert state: [?v.GetID], [?v.GetName]"
        }
        set_temp_variable = { num_of_military_factories_to_desert = num_of_military_factories }
        set_temp_variable = { num_of_civilian_factories_to_desert = num_of_civilian_factories }
        divide_temp_variable = {
            var = num_of_military_factories_to_desert
            value = num_of_owned_desert_states
        }
        divide_temp_variable = {
            var = num_of_civilian_factories_to_desert
            value = num_of_owned_desert_states
        }
        add_to_temp_variable = { slots = num_of_military_factories_to_desert }
        add_to_temp_variable = { slots = num_of_civilian_factories_to_desert }
        every_owned_state = { limit = { is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT is_desert_state = yes }
        add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = slots
        add_building_construction = {
            type = arms_factory
            level = num_of_military_factories_to_desert
            instant_build = yes
        }
        add_building_construction = {
            type = industrial_complex
            level = num_of_civilian_factories_to_desert
            instant_build = yes
        }
    }
    every_owned_state = { limit = { is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT is_desert_state = no }
    remove_building = {
        type = arms_factory
        level = 10
    }
    remove_building = {
        type = industrial_complex
        level = 10
    }
}
}
news_event = { id = chaosx.news.27 days = 2 }

}
option = {
    ai_chance = { base = 0 }
    name = chaosx.nr26.2.b
}
}

        ai_chance = { base = 25 }

        set_technology = {
            mobile_warfare = 1
            delay = 1
            elastic_defence = 1
            armored_spearhead = 1
            schwerpunk = 1
            blitzkrieg = 1
            kampfgruppe = 1
            firebrigades = 1
            backhand_blow = 1
            modern_blitzkrieg = 1
        }
        news_event = { id = chaosx.news.28 days = 4 }
    } option = {
        ai_chance = { base = 25 }
        name = chaosx.nr27.2.b
        set_technology = {

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr28.1
    title = chaosx.nr28.1.t
    desc = chaosx.nr28.1.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_asteroid

    is_triggered_only = yes
    timeout_days = 5

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = { # Immediate block shows it's effects in event desc
            random_country = {
                limit = { num_of_controlled_states > 10 }
                set_variable = { global.asteroid_country = THIS.id }
                country_event = { id = chaosx.nr28.2 days = 8 }
                news_event = { id = chaosx.news.29 days = 2 }
                random_other_country = {
                    limit = { num_of_controlled_states > 10 NOT = { tag = PREV } }
                    set_variable = { global.rand_country_1 = THIS.id }
                    random_other_country = {
                        limit = { num_of_controlled_states > 10 NOT = { OR = { tag = PREV tag = PREV.PREV } } }
                        set_variable = { global.rand_country_2 = THIS.id }
                    }
                }
            }
            random_list = { # So that the right option's position is random everytime
                33 = { set_country_flag = asteroid_location_options_1 }
                33 = { set_country_flag = asteroid_location_options_2 }
                33 = { set_country_flag = asteroid_location_options_3 }
            }
        }
    }

    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr28.1.a
        hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = asteroid_location_guessed }
        trigger = {
            has_country_flag = asteroid_location_options_1
        }
    } option = {
        name = chaosx.nr28.1.b
        trigger = {
            has_country_flag = asteroid_location_options_1
        }
    } option = {
        name = chaosx.nr28.1.c
        trigger = {
            has_country_flag = asteroid_location_options_1
        }
    }

        name = chaosx.nr28.1.e

            has_country_flag = asteroid_location_options_2
        }
    } option = {
        name = chaosx.nr28.1.f

        trigger = {
            has_country_flag = asteroid_location_options_2
        }
    } option = {
        name = chaosx.nr28.1.g

            has_country_flag = asteroid_location_options_2
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr28.1.h
        trigger = {
            has_country_flag = asteroid_location_options_3
        }
    } option = {
        name = chaosx.nr28.1.i

            has_country_flag = asteroid_location_options_3

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr28.2
    title = chaosx.nr28.2.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        clear_variable = global.rand_country_1
        clear_variable = global.rand_country_2
        if = { limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = asteroid_location_guessed } }
        ROOT = { # Less manpower loss and industry evacuation
            news_event = { id = chaosx.news.30 days = 3 }
            news_event = { id = chaosx.news.32 days = 1 }
            FROM = { add_timed_idea = { idea = asteroid_prediction_correct years = 1 } }
            add_opinion_modifier = {
                target = FROM
                modifier = cheat_opinion_modifier_good
            }
            random_owned_state = {
                ROOT = {
                    launch_nuke = {
                        state = PREV
                        controller = ROOT
                        use_nuke = no
                    }
                }
                every_country = {
                    limit = { is_ai = no }
                    goto_state = PREV # Moves camera to the specified state
                }
                remove_building = {
                    type = arms_factory
                    level = 1
                } remove_building = {
                    type = industrial_complex
                    level = 1
                } remove_building = {
                    type = infrastructure
                    level = 2
                }
                add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = -10
                every_neighbor_state = {
                    damage_building = {
                        type = arms_factory
                        damage = 1
                    }
                    damage_building = {
                        type = industrial_complex
                        damage = 1
                    }
                    damage_building = {
                        type = infrastructure
                        damage = 1
                    }
                    add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = -3
                    every_neighbor_state = {
                        add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = -1
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    } else = {
        ROOT = {
            news_event = { id = chaosx.news.32 days = 2 }
            add_opinion_modifier = {
                target = FROM
                modifier = hostile_status
            }
            random_owned_state = {
                add_manpower = -100000
                ROOT = {
                    launch_nuke = {
                        state = PREV
                        controller = ROOT
                        use_nuke = no
                    }
                }
                every_country = {
                    limit = { is_ai = no }
                    goto_state = PREV # Moves camera to the specified state
                }
                remove_building = {
                    type = arms_factory
                    level = 10
                } remove_building = {
                    type = industrial_complex
                    level = 10
                } remove_building = {
                    type = infrastructure
                    level = 5
                }
                add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = -10
                every_neighbor_state = {
                    add_manpower = -10000
                    remove_building = {
                        type = arms_factory
                        level = 2
                    } remove_building = {
                        type = industrial_complex
                        level = 2
                    } remove_building = {
                        type = infrastructure
                        level = 2
                    }
                    damage_building = {
                        type = arms_factory
                        damage = 2
                    }
                    damage_building = {
                        type = industrial_complex
                        damage = 2
                    }
                    damage_building = {
                        type = infrastructure
                        damage = 3
                    }
                    add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = -3
                    every_neighbor_state = {
                        add_manpower = -1000
                        damage_building = {
                            type = infrastructure
                            damage = 3
                        }
                        damage_building = {
                            type = industrial_complex
                            damage = 2
                        }
                        damage_building = {
                            type = infrastructure
                            damage = 3
                        }
                        add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = -1
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
}

    title = chaosx.nr32.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        every_country = {
            country_event = { id = chaosx.nr32.2 days = 1 }
            set_technology = {
                experimental_rockets = 1
                rocket_engines = 1
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    NOT = {
                        has_built = { # When the event has been fired already, then use random states other than capital. 2 rocket sites per state
                            type = rocket_site
                            value > 1
                        }
                    }
                }
                capital_scope = {
                    add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
                    add_building_construction = {
                        type = rocket_site
                        level = 2
                        instant_build = yes
                    }
                }
            } else = {
                random_owned_state = {
                    limit = {
                        NOT = {
                            rocket_site > 1
                        }
                    }
                    add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
                    add_building_construction = {
                        type = rocket_site
                        level = 2
                        instant_build = yes
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr33.1
    title = chaosx.nr33.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            news_event = { id = chaosx.news.37 days = 2 }
            random_list = {
                10 = {
                    set_variable = { global.acid_rain_continent = 1 }
                    add_to_array = { global.acid_rain_continents = global.acid_rain_continent }
                    get_num_states_in_continent = yes
                    every_state = {
                        limit = { is_on_continent = europe }
                        add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_clouds_state days = global.acid_clouds_time }
                    }
                    random_state = {
                        limit = { is_on_continent = europe }
                        add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state days = 14 }
                        every_neighbor_state = {
                            limit = { is_on_continent = europe }
                            add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state days = 14 }
                        }
                    }
                    every_country = {
                        limit = { any_owned_state = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state } } }
                        country_event = { id = chaosx.nr33.2 days = 1 }
                    }
                } 10 = {
                    set_variable = { global.acid_rain_continent = 2 }
                    add_to_array = { global.acid_rain_continents = global.acid_rain_continent }
                    get_num_states_in_continent = yes
                    every_state = {
                        limit = { is_on_continent = middle_east }
                        add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_clouds_state days = global.acid_clouds_time }
                    }
                    random_state = {
                        limit = { is_on_continent = middle_east }
                        add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state days = 14 }
                        every_neighbor_state = {
                            limit = { is_on_continent = middle_east }
                            add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state days = 14 }
                        }
                    }
                    every_country = {
                        limit = { any_owned_state = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state } } }
                        country_event = { id = chaosx.nr33.2 days = 1 }
                    }
                } 10 = {
                    set_variable = { global.acid_rain_continent = 3 }
                    add_to_array = { global.acid_rain_continents = global.acid_rain_continent }
                    get_num_states_in_continent = yes
                    every_state = {
                        limit = { is_on_continent = asia }
                        add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_clouds_state days = global.acid_clouds_time }
                    }
                    random_state = {
                        limit = { is_on_continent = asia }
                        add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state days = 14 }
                        every_neighbor_state = {
                            limit = { is_on_continent = asia }
                            add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state days = 14 }
                        }
                    }
                    every_country = {
                        limit = { any_owned_state = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state } } }
                        country_event = { id = chaosx.nr33.2 days = 1 }
                    }
                } 10 = {
                    set_variable = { global.acid_rain_continent = 4 }
                    add_to_array = { global.acid_rain_continents = global.acid_rain_continent }
                    get_num_states_in_continent = yes
                    every_state = {
                        limit = { is_on_continent = africa }
                        add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_clouds_state days = global.acid_clouds_time }
                    }
                    random_state = {
                        limit = { is_on_continent = africa }
                        add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state days = 14 }
                        every_neighbor_state = {
                            limit = { is_on_continent = africa }
                            add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state days = 14 }
                        }
                    }
                    every_country = {
                        limit = { any_owned_state = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state } } }
                        country_event = { id = chaosx.nr33.2 days = 1 }
                    }
                } 10 = {
                    set_variable = { global.acid_rain_continent = 5 }
                    add_to_array = { global.acid_rain_continents = global.acid_rain_continent }
                    get_num_states_in_continent = yes
                    every_state = {
                        limit = { is_on_continent = australia }
                        add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_clouds_state days = global.acid_clouds_time }
                    }
                    random_state = {
                        limit = { is_on_continent = australia }
                        add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state days = 14 }
                        every_neighbor_state = {
                            limit = { is_on_continent = australia }
                            add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state days = 14 }
                        }
                    }
                    every_country = {
                        limit = { any_owned_state = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state } } }
                        country_event = { id = chaosx.nr33.2 days = 1 }
                    }
                } 10 = {
                    set_variable = { global.acid_rain_continent = 6 }
                    add_to_array = { global.acid_rain_continents = global.acid_rain_continent }
                    get_num_states_in_continent = yes
                    every_state = {
                        limit = { is_on_continent = north_america }
                        add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_clouds_state days = global.acid_clouds_time }
                    }
                    random_state = {
                        limit = { is_on_continent = north_america }
                        add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state days = 14 }
                        every_neighbor_state = {
                            limit = { is_on_continent = north_america }
                            add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state days = 14 }
                        }
                    }
                    every_country = {
                        limit = { any_owned_state = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state } } }
                        country_event = { id = chaosx.nr33.2 days = 1 }
                    }
                } 10 = {
                    set_variable = { global.acid_rain_continent = 7 }
                    add_to_array = { global.acid_rain_continents = global.acid_rain_continent }
                    get_num_states_in_continent = yes
                    every_state = {
                        limit = { is_on_continent = south_america }
                        add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_clouds_state days = global.acid_clouds_time }
                    }
                    random_state = {
                        limit = { is_on_continent = south_america }
                        add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state days = 14 }
                        every_neighbor_state = {
                            limit = { is_on_continent = south_america }
                            add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state days = 14 }
                        }
                    }
                    every_country = {
                        limit = { any_owned_state = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state } } }
                        country_event = { id = chaosx.nr33.2 days = 1 }
                    }
                }
            }
            set_global_flag = acid_rain
            activate_mission = chaosx_acid_rain_timeout
            activate_mission = chaosx_acid_clouds_timeout
        }
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr38.1
    title = chaosx.nr38.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes


    immediate = {
        every_country = {
            limit = { any_owned_state = { is_core_of = MLT } }
            release = MLT
        }
        news_event = { id = chaosx.news.43 days = 2 }
        MLT = {
            set_cosmetic_tag = CRU
            add_ideas = ninth_crusade
            add_war_support = 1.00
            add_stability = 1.00
            set_politics = {
                ruling_party = neutrality
                elections_allowed = no
                election_frequency = 48
                long_name = "The Ninth Crusade Order"
                name = "Crusaders"
            }
            add_popularity = {
                ideology = neutrality
                popularity = 1.00
            }
            retire_country_leader = yes
            create_country_leader = {
                name = "The Leader of the Order of Malta"
                picture = GFX_portrait_CRU_crusader
                ideology = despotism
            }
            set_technology = {
                artillery1 = 1
                tech_support = 1
                tech_engineers = 1
                tech_recon = 1
                tech_maintenance_company = 1
                infantry_weapons1 = 1
            }
            add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
                type = convoy
                amount = 200
            }

        }
        every_state = {
            limit = { OR = { state = 677 state = 344 state = 350 state = 553 state = 454 state = 799 state = 183 state = 182 state = 455 is_core_of = GRE is_core_of = TUR state = 453 state = 446 } }
            add_core_of = MLT
        }
        every_state = {
            limit = { OR = { state = 183 state = 797 state = 182 state = 47 state = 454 state = 553 state = 799 state = 677 state = 344 state = 345 } }
            transfer_state_to = MLT
        }

        MLT = {
            division_template = {
                name = "Malta Knights Division"
                regiments = {
                    irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
                    irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
                    irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
                    irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 3 }
                    irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
                    irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
                    irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
                    irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 3 }
                    irregular_infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
                    irregular_infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
                    irregular_infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
                    irregular_infantry = { x = 2 y = 3 }
                    irregular_infantry = { x = 3 y = 0 }
                    irregular_infantry = { x = 3 y = 1 }
                    irregular_infantry = { x = 3 y = 2 }
                    irregular_infantry = { x = 3 y = 3 }
                }
                support = {
                    recon = { x = 0 y = 0 }
                    maintenance_company = { x = 0 y = 1 }
                    engineer = { x = 0 y = 2 }
                    artillery = { x = 0 y = 3 }
                }
            }
            every_owned_state = {
                create_unit = {
                    division = "name = \"The Crusaders\" division_template = \"Malta Knights Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
                    count = 2
                    owner = MLT
                }
            }
        }
        every_country = {
            limit = { any_owned_state = { is_core_of = MLT }  }
            MLT = {
                declare_war_on = {
                    type = take_core_state
                    target = PREV
                }
            }
            country_event = { id = chaosx.nr38.2 days = 1 }
        }
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr41.1
    title = chaosx.nr41.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        if = { limit = { any_country = { has_war = yes num_divisions > 10 } }
        random_country = {
            limit = {
                has_war = yes
                num_divisions > 10
            }
            every_country = {
                limit = { is_neighbor_of = PREV }
                PREV = {
                    every_owned_state = {
                        limit = { any_neighbor_state = { is_controlled_by = PREV.PREV } }
                        damage_units = {
                            state = THIS
                            limit = { always = no }
                            org_damage = 0.5
                            str_damage = 0.5
                            ratio = yes
                            army = yes
                            navy = no
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            country_event = { id = chaosx.nr41.2 days = 1 }
        }
    } else = {
        every_owned_state = {
            limit = { has_ROOT_at_least_1_div_in_current_state_scope = yes } # Probably unnecessary
            damage_units = {
                state = THIS
                limit = { always = no }
                org_damage = 0.5
                str_damage = 0.5
                ratio = yes
                army = yes
                navy = no
            }
        }

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr52.1
    title = chaosx.nr52.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        if = { limit = { any_country = { OR = { is_major = yes is_ai = no } has_war = yes } }
        random_country = {
            limit = { OR = { is_major = yes is_ai = no } has_war = yes }
            country_event = { id = chaosx.nr52.2 }
        }
    } else = {
        country_event = { id = chaosx.nr52.2 }
    }
}
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr53.1
    title = chaosx.nr53.1.t
    desc = chaosx.nr53.1.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_mysterious_man

    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr53.1.a
        add_political_power = -200
    }
    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr53.1.b
        add_political_power = 50
        hidden_effect = {
            random_list = {
                10 = { add_research_slot = -2 }
                10 = { capital_scope = { ROOT = { launch_nuke = { state = PREV controller = ROOT } goto_state = PREV } } }
                10 = {
                    modifier = { factor = 0 all_controlled_state = { is_core_of = ROOT } }
                    every_controlled_state = {
                        limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT } }
                        add_resistance = 100
                    }
                }
                10 = { add_war_support = -0.5 add_stability = -0.5 }
                10 = { random_country = { limit = { is_major = no } ROOT = { inherit_technology = PREV } } }
                10 = { set_fuel = 0 }
                10 = {
                    start_civil_war = {
                        ideology = fascism
                        size = 0.4
                    }
                }
                10 = {
                    every_owned_state = {
                        remove_building = {
                            type = arms_factory
                            level = 1
                        }
                    }
                }
                10 = {
                    every_owned_state = {
                        remove_building = {
                            type = industrial_complex
                            level = 1
                        }
                    }
                }
                10 = {
                    every_owned_state = {
                        damage_building = {
                            type = industrial_complex
                            damage = 0.20
                        } damage_building = {
                            type = arms_factory
                            damage = 0.20
                        } damage_building = {
                            type = infrastructure
                            damage = 1.00
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

    }
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr55.1
    title = chaosx.nr55.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        random_country = {
            limit = { check_variable = { num_owned_states > 10 } } # check_variable is needed since there is no trigger for the variable
            country_event = { id = chaosx.nr55.2 }
        }
    }
}


##############################################################################################################


country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr55.2
    title = chaosx.nr55.2.t
    desc = chaosx.nr55.2.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_infrastructure_project

    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr55.2.a
        news_event = { id = chaosx.news.54 days = 2 }
        every_owned_state = {
            add_building_construction = {
                type = infrastructure
                level = 5
                instant_build = yes
            }
        }

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr56.2
    title = chaosx.nr56.2.t
    desc = chaosx.nr56.2.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_ast_navy

    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr56.2.a
        create_equipment_variant = {
            allow_without_tech = yes
            name = "Destroyer Class"
            type = ship_hull_light_2
            role_icon_index = auto
            modules = {
                fixed_ship_battery_slot = ship_light_battery_1
                fixed_ship_anti_air_slot = ship_anti_air_1
                fixed_ship_fire_control_system_slot = ship_fire_control_system_0
                fixed_ship_radar_slot = empty
                fixed_ship_engine_slot = light_ship_engine_2
                fixed_ship_torpedo_slot = ship_torpedo_1
                mid_1_custom_slot = ship_mine_layer_1
                rear_1_custom_slot = ship_depth_charge_1
            }
        }
        for_loop_effect = {
            end = 20
            create_ship = {
                type = ship_hull_light_2
                equipment_variant = "Destroyer Class"
            }
        }
        create_equipment_variant = {
            allow_without_tech = yes
            name = "Submarine Class"
            type = ship_hull_submarine_2
            role_icon_index = auto
            modules = {
                fixed_ship_torpedo_slot = ship_torpedo_sub_2
                fixed_ship_engine_slot = sub_ship_engine_2
                rear_1_custom_slot = ship_torpedo_sub_2
            }
        }
        for_loop_effect = {
            end = 50
            create_ship = {
                type = ship_hull_submarine_2
                equipment_variant = "Submarine Class"
            }
        }
        create_equipment_variant = {
            allow_without_tech = yes
            name = "Cruiser Class"
            type = ship_hull_cruiser_2
            role_icon_index = auto
            modules = {
                fixed_ship_battery_slot = ship_light_medium_battery_1
                fixed_ship_anti_air_slot = ship_anti_air_2
                fixed_ship_fire_control_system_slot = ship_fire_control_system_0
                fixed_ship_radar_slot = empty
                fixed_ship_engine_slot = cruiser_ship_engine_2
                fixed_ship_armor_slot = ship_armor_cruiser_2
                fixed_ship_secondaries_slot = dp_ship_secondaries_1
                mid_1_custom_slot = ship_torpedo_1
                mid_2_custom_slot = ship_torpedo_1
                rear_1_custom_slot = ship_light_medium_battery_1
            }
        }
        for_loop_effect = {
            end = 3
            create_ship = {
                type = ship_hull_cruiser_2
                equipment_variant = "Cruiser Class"
            }
        }
        create_equipment_variant = {
            allow_without_tech = yes
            name = "Battleship Class"
            type = ship_hull_heavy_2
            role_icon_index = auto
            modules = {
                fixed_ship_battery_slot = ship_heavy_battery_1
                fixed_ship_anti_air_slot = ship_anti_air_2
                fixed_ship_fire_control_system_slot = ship_fire_control_system_1
                fixed_ship_radar_slot = empty
                fixed_ship_engine_slot = heavy_ship_engine_1
                fixed_ship_secondaries_slot = dp_ship_secondaries_1
                fixed_ship_armor_slot = ship_armor_bb_1
                front_1_custom_slot = ship_heavy_battery_1
                mid_1_custom_slot = ship_anti_air_2
                mid_2_custom_slot = dp_ship_secondaries_1
                rear_1_custom_slot = ship_heavy_battery_1
            }
        }
        create_ship = {
            type = ship_hull_heavy_2
            equipment_variant = "Battleship Class"
        }create_ship = {
            type = ship_hull_heavy_2
            equipment_variant = "Battleship Class"
        }
        create_equipment_variant = {
            allow_without_tech = yes
            name = "Carrier Class"
            type = ship_hull_carrier_2
            role_icon_index = auto
            modules = {
                fixed_ship_deck_slot_1 = ship_deck_space
                fixed_ship_deck_slot_2 = ship_deck_space
                fixed_ship_anti_air_slot = ship_anti_air_2
                fixed_ship_radar_slot = empty
                fixed_ship_engine_slot = carrier_ship_engine_3
                fixed_ship_secondaries_slot = ship_secondaries_1
                front_1_custom_slot = ship_deck_space
            }
        }
        create_ship = {
            type = ship_hull_carrier_2
            equipment_variant = "Carrier Class"
        }
        ai_chance = { base = 100 }
    }

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr57.2
    title = chaosx.nr57.2.t
    desc = chaosx.nr57.2.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_radar_01

    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr57.2.a
        set_technology = {
            decimetric_radar = 1
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                NOT = {
                    has_built = {
                        type = radar_station
                        value > 1
                    }
                }
            }
            capital_scope = { # The first time is going to be at the capital
                add_building_construction = {
                    type = radar_station
                    level = 6
                    instant_build = yes
                }
            }
        } else = {
            random_owned_state = {
                limit = {
                    NOT = {
                        radar_station > 1
                    }
                }
                add_building_construction = {
                    type = radar_station
                    level = 6
                    instant_build = yes
                }
            }
        }
        ai_chance = { base = 100 }
    }
}

                level = mils_to_convert

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr62.1
    title = chaosx.nr62.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        if = { limit = { any_country = { is_subject = no is_in_faction_with = ENG is_major = no } }
        random_country = {
            limit = { is_subject = no is_in_faction_with = ENG is_major = no }
            country_event = { id = chaosx.nr62.2 }
        }
    } else = {
        random_country = {
            limit = { is_faction_leader = yes num_faction_members > 1 }
            random_country = {
                limit = { is_subject = no is_in_faction_with = PREV }
                country_event = { id = chaosx.nr62.3 }
            }
        }
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr65.1
    title = chaosx.nr65.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        every_country = {
            country_event = { id = chaosx.nr65.2 }
        }
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr66.1
    title = chaosx.nr66.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        random_country = {
            limit = { OR = { is_major = yes is_ai = no } }
            country_event = { id = chaosx.nr66.2 }
        }
    }
}


##############################################################################################################


country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr66.2
    title = chaosx.nr66.2.t
    desc = chaosx.nr66.2.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_tank_factory

    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr66.2.a
        add_cic = 100000
        news_event = { id = chaosx.news.58 days = 2 }
        ai_chance = { base = 100 }
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr67.1
    title = chaosx.nr67.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        random_country = {
            limit = { OR = { is_major = yes is_ai = no } }
            set_variable = { global.generalissimo_country = THIS.id }
            random_army_leader = {
                unit_leader_event = { id = chaosx.nr67.2 }
                set_variable = { global.generalissimo = THIS.id }
            }
        }
    }
}

                    add_core_of = ZIN
                }
            }
        }
    }
    ai_chance = {
        factor = 0
        modifier = {
            add = 10
            any_country = { NOT = { tag = ZIN } has_war_with = ROOT }
        }
        modifier = {
            add = 10
            has_stability < 0.5
            has_war_support < 0.5
        }
        modifier = {
            add = 20
            has_stability < 0.25
            has_war_support < 0.25
        }
        modifier = {
            add = 20
            has_stability < 0.10
            has_war_support < 0.10
        }
        modifier = {
            add = 20
            has_manpower < 10000
        }
        modifier = {
            add = 5
            has_damaged_buildings = yes
        }
        modifier = {
            add = 15
            all_owned_state = {
                OR = {
                    non_damaged_building_level = {
                        building = arms_factory
                        level < 2
                    }
                    non_damaged_building_level = {
                        building = industrial_complex
                        level < 2
                    }
                    non_damaged_building_level = {
                        building = infrastructure
                        level < 2
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr77.1
    title = chaosx.nr77.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        random_country = {
            limit = {
                OR = { is_major = yes is_ai = no }
                OR = {
                    # Infantry
                    has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > 1000 }
                    has_equipment = { artillery_equipment > 150 }
                    has_equipment = { anti_air_equipment > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { anti_tank_equipment > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { support_equipment > 200 }
                    # Motorized/Supply
                    has_equipment = { motorized_equipment > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { armored_car_equipment > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { mechanized_equipment > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { amphibious_mechanized_equipment > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { train_equipment > 10 }
                    has_equipment = { convoy > 100 }
                    # Planes
                    has_equipment = { small_plane_airframe > 50 }
                    has_equipment = { cv_small_plane_airframe > 50 }
                    has_equipment = { small_plane_cas_airframe > 50 }
                    has_equipment = { cv_small_plane_cas_airframe > 50 }
                    has_equipment = { small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe > 50 }
                    has_equipment = { cv_small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe > 50 }
                    has_equipment = { small_plane_suicide_airframe > 50 }
                    has_equipment = { cv_small_plane_suicide_airframe > 50 }
                    has_equipment = { jet_fighter_equipment > 50 }
                    has_equipment = { rocket_interceptor_equipment > 50 }
                    has_equipment = { medium_plane_airframe > 50 }
                    has_equipment = { medium_plane_fighter_airframe > 50 }
                    has_equipment = { medium_plane_scout_plane_airframe > 50 }
                    has_equipment = { jet_tac_bomber_equipment > 50 }
                    has_equipment = { large_plane_airframe > 50 }
                    has_equipment = { large_plane_maritime_patrol_plane_airframe > 50 }
                    has_equipment = { jet_strat_bomber_equipment > 50 }
                    has_equipment = { transport_plane_equipment > 50 }
                    # Tanks
                    has_equipment = { light_tank_chassis > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { light_tank_aa_chassis > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { light_tank_artillery_chassis > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { light_tank_destroyer_chassis > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { light_tank_amphibious_chassis > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { light_tank_flame_chassis > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { medium_tank_chassis > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { medium_tank_aa_chassis > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { medium_tank_artillery_chassis > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { medium_tank_destroyer_chassis > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { medium_tank_amphibious_chassis > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { medium_tank_flame_chassis > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { heavy_tank_chassis > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { heavy_tank_chassis > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { heavy_tank_aa_chassis > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { heavy_tank_artillery_chassis > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { heavy_tank_destroyer_chassis > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { heavy_tank_amphibious_chassis > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { heavy_tank_flame_chassis > 100 }
                    # Late game
                    has_equipment = { modern_tank_chassis > 50 }
                    has_equipment = { super_heavy_tank_chassis > 50 }
                    has_equipment = { amphibious_tank_chassis > 100 }
                    has_equipment = { railway_gun_equipment > 1 }
                }
            }
            # Get random minors
            random_other_country = {
                limit = { is_major = no NOT = { is_ally_with = PREV } is_in_faction = no is_subject = no }
                set_variable = { global.random_minor_1 = THIS.id }
                random_other_country = {
                    limit = { is_major = no NOT = { is_ally_with = PREV.PREV } is_in_faction = no is_subject = no }
                    set_variable = { global.random_minor_2 = THIS.id }
                    random_other_country = {
                        limit = { is_major = no NOT = { is_ally_with = PREV.PREV.PREV tag = PREV.PREV } is_in_faction = no is_subject = no }
                        set_variable = { global.random_minor_3 = THIS.id }
                    }
                }
            }

            country_event = { id = chaosx.nr77.3 }
        }
    }
}

    id = chaosx.nr78.2
    title = chaosx.nr78.1.t
    desc = chaosx.nr78.1.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_SOV_mongolia_fortify_border

    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            random_other_country = {
                limit = { is_neighbor_of = ROOT NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT } }
                set_variable = { global.border_war_country = PREV.id }
            }
        }
    }

    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr78.2.a
        add_war_support = 0.10
        add_political_power = 50
        var:global.border_war_country = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr78.3 days = 5 } }
        news_event = { id = chaosx.news.78 days = 2 }
        ai_chance = { base = 100 }
    }
    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr78.2.b
        add_war_support = -0.20
        add_political_power = -100
        declare_war_on = {
            type = annex_everything
            target = global.border_war_country
        }
        ai_chance = { base = 0 }
    }
}
