    id = chaosx.nr78.3
    title = chaosx.nr78.3.t
    desc = chaosx.nr78.3.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_SOV_mongolia_fortify_border

    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr78.3.a
        every_owned_state = {
            limit = { any_neighbor_state = { is_controlled_by = FROM } }
            FROM = {
                every_owned_state = {
                    limit = { any_neighbor_state = { is_controlled_by = ROOT } }
                    FROM = {
                        start_border_war = {
                            change_state_after_war = yes
                            attacker = {
                                state = PREV.PREV.PREV
                                num_provinces = 100 # just to make sure all the provinces are used
                                on_win = chaosx.nr78.4
                                on_lose = chaosx.nr78.5
                                on_cancel = chaosx.nr78.6
                            }
                            defender = {
                                state = PREV
                                num_provinces = 100
                                on_win = chaosx.nr78.4
                                on_lose = chaosx.nr78.5
                                on_cancel = chaosx.nr78.6
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr79.1
    title = chaosx.nr79.1.t
    desc = chaosx.nr79.1.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_hitler_handshake

    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            set_country_flag = fight_for_minor
            random_other_country = {
                limit = { is_major = no num_of_factories < ROOT.num_of_factories has_war = no is_in_faction = no }
                set_variable = { global.minor_to_attract = THIS.id }
                ROOT = { give_guarantee = PREV }
                every_country = {
                    limit = { is_enemy_ideology = yes OR = { is_major = yes num_of_factories > ROOT.num_of_factories } }
                    set_country_flag = fight_for_minor
                    give_guarantee = PREV
                }
            }
            every_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = fight_for_minor } add_to_array = { global.masters_array = THIS.id } }
        }
    }

    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr79.1.a
        add_political_power = 50
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr79.2
    title = chaosx.nr79.2.t
    desc = chaosx.nr79.2.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_hitler_handshake

    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr79.2.a
        every_country = {
            limit = { has_guaranteed = var:global.minor_to_attract }
            meta_effect = {
                text = {
                    diplomatic_relation = {
                        country = [MINOR_TO_ATTRACT]
                        relation = guarantee
                        active = no
                    }
                }
                MINOR_TO_ATTRACT = "[?global.minor_to_attract.GetID]"
            }
        }
        puppet = {
            target = var:global.minor_to_attract
            end_wars = yes
        }
        news_event = { id = chaosx.news.66 days = 1 }
    }

}

    title = chaosx.nr80.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes


    immediate = {
        USA = {
            country_event = { id = chaosx.nr80.3 }
            set_country_flag = airship_country
        }
        set_global_flag = airship
        activate_mission = airship_timeout
        set_variable = { global.airship_d = 0 }
        every_country = {
            limit = { NOT = { tag = USA } }
            country_event = { id = chaosx.nr80.2 days = 2 }
            set_variable = { as_crash_chance = 1 } # 1 out of 100 as base
        }
    }
}

        add_political_power = -50
        add_stability = -0.05
        add_timed_idea = {
            idea = british_tax
            years = 1
        }
        ENG = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr81.5 days = 1 } }
        ai_chance = { base = 60 }
        name = chaosx.nr81.3.a
    }
    option = {
        add_political_power = 50
        add_war_support = 0.05
        ENG = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr81.4 days = 1 } }
        name = chaosx.nr81.3.b
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 40
            modifier = {
                add = 20
                has_opinion = {
                    target = ENG
                    value < 0
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                add = 20
                ENG = { is_enemy_ideology = yes }
            }
            modifier = {
                add = 60
                is_major = yes
            }
        }
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr89.1
    title = chaosx.nr89.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes


    immediate = {
        every_country = {
            limit = { OR = { tag = ENG tag = SOV tag = GER tag = JAP } }

            if = { limit = { tag = ENG }
            add_to_tech_sharing_group = chaosx_research_group_1
        } else_if = { limit = { tag = SOV }
        add_to_tech_sharing_group = chaosx_research_group_2
    }else_if = { limit = { tag = GER }
    add_to_tech_sharing_group = chaosx_research_group_3
}else_if = { limit = { tag = JAP }
add_to_tech_sharing_group = chaosx_research_group_4
}
country_event = { id = chaosx.nr89.3 }
}
every_country = {
    limit = { NOT = { OR = { tag = ENG tag = SOV tag = GER tag = JAP } } }
    country_event = { id = chaosx.nr89.2 }
}
}
}


##############################################################################################################


country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr89.2
    title = chaosx.nr89.2.t
    desc = chaosx.nr89.2.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_generic_research_lab

    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        add_to_tech_sharing_group = chaosx_research_group_1
        ENG = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr89.4 } }
        add_opinion_modifier = {
            target = ENG
            modifier = small_increase
        }
        name = chaosx.nr89.2.a
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 5
            modifier = {
                add = 100
                OR = {
                    has_government = ENG
                    is_in_faction_with = ENG
                }
            }
        }
        trigger = {
            NOT = { has_war_with = ENG }
        }
    }
    option = {
        add_to_tech_sharing_group = chaosx_research_group_2
        SOV = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr89.4 } }
        add_opinion_modifier = {
            target = SOV
            modifier = small_increase
        }
        name = chaosx.nr89.2.b
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 5
            modifier = {
                add = 100
                has_government = SOV
            }
        }
        trigger = {
            NOT = { has_war_with = SOV }
        }
    }
    option = {
        add_to_tech_sharing_group = chaosx_research_group_3
        GER = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr89.4 } }
        add_opinion_modifier = {
            target = GER
            modifier = small_increase
        }
        name = chaosx.nr89.2.c
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 5
            modifier = {
                add = 100
                has_government = GER
                NOT = { capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia } }
            }
        }
        trigger = {
            NOT = { has_war_with = GER }
            NOT = { ROOT = { capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia } } }
        }
    }
    option = {
        add_to_tech_sharing_group = chaosx_research_group_4
        JAP = { country_event = { id = chaosx.nr89.4 } }
        add_opinion_modifier = {
            target = JAP
            modifier = small_increase
        }
        name = chaosx.nr89.2.e
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 5
            modifier = {
                add = 100
                has_government = JAP
                capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia }
            }
        }
        trigger = {
            NOT = { has_war_with = JAP }
            ROOT = { capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia } }
        }
    }

    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr89.2.g
        ai_chance = { base = 10 }

    }
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr91.1
    title = chaosx.nr91.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes


    immediate = {
        random_state = {
            set_temp_variable = { REV.temp_oob_container = owner.id }
            transfer_state_to = REV
        }
        REV = { load_oob = "REV_1936" create_faction = revolution_front } # if country doesn't exist, does nothing
        every_state = {
            limit = { is_owned_by = REV }
            transfer_state_to = REV.temp_oob_container
        }
        every_state = {
            limit = { is_core_of = SOV }
            add_claim_by = REV
        }
        every_country = {
            limit = { NOT = { has_government = communism } }
            country_event = { id = chaosx.nr91.2 }
        }
        every_country = {
            limit = { has_government = communism }
            country_event = { id = chaosx.nr91.3 }
        }
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr91.2
    title = chaosx.nr91.2.t
    desc = chaosx.nr91.2.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_lenin

    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            set_temp_variable = { rand_communist_states = party_popularity@communism }
            multiply_temp_variable = { rand_communist_states = num_owned_states }
            round_temp_variable = rand_communist_states
            if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { rand_communist_states = 0 } } }
            meta_effect = {
                text = {
                    every_owned_state = {
                        limit = { impassable = no }
                        random_select_amount = [COMMUNIST_STATES_AMOUNT] # doesn't allow normal variable input
                        transfer_state_to = REV
                        add_core_of = REV
                        if = { limit = { is_on_continent = middle_east }
                        create_unit = {
                            division = "name = \"Revolutinaries of Arabia\" division_template = \"Regular Revolutionary Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
                            owner = REV
                            count = 1
                            allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
                        }
                        create_unit = {
                            division = "name = \"Believers of the Cause\" division_template = \"Red Army Irregulars\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
                            owner = REV
                            count = 2
                            allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
                        }
                        create_unit = {
                            division = "name = \"Red Camels\" division_template = \"Red Army Cavalry\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
                            owner = REV
                            count = 1
                            allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
                        }
                    } else_if = { limit = { is_on_continent = asia }
                    create_unit = {
                        division = "name = \"Revolutionaries\" division_template = \"Regular Revolutionary Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
                        owner = REV
                        count = 1
                        allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
                    }
                    create_unit = {
                        division = "name = \"Belivers of the Cause\" division_template = \"Red Army Irregulars\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
                        owner = REV
                        count = 1
                        allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
                    }
                    create_unit = {
                        division = "name = \"Red Cossacks\" division_template = \"Red Army Cavalry\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
                        owner = REV
                        count = 2
                        allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
                    }
                } else_if = { limit = { is_on_continent = south_america }
                create_unit = {
                    division = "name = \"Revolucionarios\" division_template = \"Regular Revolutionary Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
                    owner = REV
                    count = 2
                    allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
                }
                create_unit = {
                    division = "name = \"Creyentes de la Causa\" division_template = \"Red Army Irregulars\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
                    owner = REV
                    count = 1
                    allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
                }
                create_unit = {
                    division = "name = \"Cosacos Rojos\" division_template = \"Red Army Cavalry\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
                    owner = REV
                    count = 1
                    allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
                }
            } else = {
                create_unit = {
                    division = "name = \"Revolutionaries\" division_template = \"Regular Revolutionary Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
                    owner = REV
                    count = 2
                    allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
                }
                create_unit = {
                    division = "name = \"The Red Army\" division_template = \"Red Army Infantry\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
                    owner = REV
                    count = 2
                    allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
                }
                create_unit = {
                    division = "name = \"Guards of Lenin\" division_template = \"Lenin's Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.3"
                    owner = REV
                    count = 1
                    allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
                }
                create_unit = {
                    division = "name = \"Red Cossacks\" division_template = \"Red Army Cavalry\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
                    owner = REV
                    count = 1
                    allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
                }
            }
        }
    }
    COMMUNIST_STATES_AMOUNT = "[?rand_communist_states|.0]"
}

}
REV = {
    declare_war_on = {
        target = ROOT
        type = annex_everything
    }
}
set_political_party = {
    ideology = communism
    popularity = 0
}
}
}
option = {
    add_war_support = 0.05
    add_political_power = 50
    name = chaosx.nr91.2.a
    ai_chance = { base = 100 }
}
}

                    irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
                    irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
                    cavalry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
                    cavalry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
                }
            }
            every_owned_state = {
                create_unit = {
                    division = "name = \"Rebels\" division_template = \"Revolt Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
                    owner = PREV
                    count = 1
                    allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
                }
            }

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr97.1
    title = chaosx.nr97.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        add_to_variable = { global.collaboration = 0.1 }
        every_country = {
            country_event = { id = chaosx.nr97.2 }
        }
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr97.2
    title = chaosx.nr97.2.t
    desc = chaosx.nr97.2.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_molotov_ribentrop_handshake

    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        every_other_country = {
            add_collaboration = {
                target = ROOT
                value = 0.1
            }
        }
        name = chaosx.nr97.2.a
        ai_chance = { base = 100 }
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr98.1
    title = chaosx.nr98.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        random_state = {
            limit = { NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = special_ore_state } } }
            set_variable = { ore_state = THIS.id }
            set_variable = { global.ore_state_container = THIS.id }
            ROOT = { goto_state = PREV }
            add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = special_ore_state } # just to indicate where the special state is
            owner = {
                country_event = { id = chaosx.nr98.2 }
                add_ideas = special_iron_ore
            }
        }
    }
}


##############################################################################################################


country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr98.2
    title = chaosx.nr98.2.t
    desc = chaosx.nr98.2.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_FIN_petsamo_mine

    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        news_event = { id = chaosx.news.77 days = 1 }
        name = chaosx.nr98.2.a
        ai_chance = { base = 100 }
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr99.1
    title = chaosx.nr99.1.t

    hidden = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            random_list = {
                10 = {
                    set_variable = { global.desert_storm_continent = 1 }
                    every_state = {
                        limit = { is_on_continent = europe }
                        add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = desert_storm days = 180 }
                    }
                }10 = {
                    set_variable = { global.desert_storm_continent = 2 }
                    every_state = {
                        limit = { is_on_continent = middle_east }
                        add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = desert_storm days = 180 }
                    }
                }10 = {
                    set_variable = { global.desert_storm_continent = 3 }
                    every_state = {
                        limit = { is_on_continent = asia }
                        add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = desert_storm days = 180 }
                    }
                }10 = {
                    set_variable = { global.desert_storm_continent = 4 }
                    every_state = {
                        limit = { is_on_continent = africa }
                        add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = desert_storm days = 180 }
                    }
                }10 = {
                    set_variable = { global.desert_storm_continent = 5 }
                    every_state = {
                        limit = { is_on_continent = australia }
                        add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = desert_storm days = 180 }
                    }
                }10 = {
                    set_variable = { global.desert_storm_continent = 6 }
                    every_state = {
                        limit = { is_on_continent = north_america }
                        add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = desert_storm days = 180 }
                    }
                }10 = {
                    set_variable = { global.desert_storm_continent = 7 }
                    every_state = {
                        limit = { is_on_continent = south_america }
                        add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = desert_storm days = 180 }
                    }
                }
            }
            country_event = { id = chaosx.nr99.2 }
        }
    }

}
country_event = {
    id = chaosx.nr99.2
    title = chaosx.nr99.2.t

    picture = GFX_report_event_sandstorm

    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        name = chaosx.nr99.2.a
        ai_chance = { base = 100 }
    }
}
